Enhanced Weapons Pre-Alpha v1.1.0

A Project by ApocNewt

This mod is meant to add to the gunplay of Borderlands without completely breaking the balance of the game.
It does this by adding sights to white rarity weapons, as well as, unlocking all the barrels that were not allowed in game (i.e. Pepperbox).
Also, Torgue and Dahl AR barrels have been interchanged. This means a Dahl AR has the chance to spawn with either a Torgue rocket barrel or a Dahl Gernade barrel and vice versa.  
The biggest change to this mod is purple teir guns and above have the slightest chance of spawning with two accessories.
Please conatct me on discord if they are any bugs or concerns that something is overpowered and should be nerfed.
Nerfed White rarity sight spawning chance
Added Etech Jakobs and Torgue Weapons
Nerfed Torgue AR barrel spawns

NOTES;
I just started this project, so I have no idea what is to come.
